       function getStatsForThemeMiniStats() {
		// Call ajax request only if data is not here.
		if ($("#upv_3629394").text() == "Loading..." ) {
			jQuery.getJSON("/stats/theme/3629394?view=json", function(json){
				jQuery("#upv_3629394").empty();
				if (json.stats &amp;&amp; json.stats.uniqueVisitors &gt;= 0) {
					jQuery("#upv_3629394").append(json.stats.uniqueVisitors);				
				} else {
					jQuery("#upv_3629394").append("Not available");
				}
			});
		}
	}

             <div class="post-title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title editable-container tooltip-on-mouse" id="postTitle_4035150143">
              <h1 class="h2 postTitleView">
               <div class="title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" itemprop="name">
                Mens Sexual Issues Affecting Their Happiness
               </div>
              </h1>
             </div>
             <div class="post-content clearfix ">
              <div class="post-image">
               <div class="thisistherealimage">
                <img alt="Mens Sexual Issues Affecting Their Happiness | Cheap ED Medications Online-kamagra100.com | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="168" id="postImage_4035150143" itemprop="image" src="http://img.scoop.it/MR589iSF0LUG4pM7VGehgDl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:224; height: 168;" width="224"/>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
               <span>
                <a href="/t/best-male-impotence-medication-online/p/4035150143/2015/01/13/men-s-sexual-issues-affecting-their-happiness">
                 January 12, 10:21 PM
                </a>
               </span>
              </div>
              <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
               <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4035150143" itemprop="description">
                <p>
                 In this current era, maintaining a healthy lovemaking session has become critical due to mens sexual health issues. There are many sexual health concerns that have spoilt the happiness of couples. It not only affects the relationship, but also affects the self esteem and confidence of men.
                </p>
                <p>
                </p>
                <p>
                 Erectile Dysfunction  An inability to maintain penile erection
                </p>
                <p>
                 <br/>
                </p>
                <p>
                 Due to  Poor blood circulation, unhealthy diet and poor lifestyle
                </p>
                <p>
                </p>
                <p>
                 Testosterone Deficiency Syndrome  Lowers level of sperm count and motility
                </p>
                <p>
                 <br/>
                </p>
                <p>
                 Due to  Erectile dysfunction, unhealthy diet etc
                </p>
                <p>
                </p>
                <p>
                 Peyronies Disease  A narrowed and curved male penile shape
                </p>
                <p>
                 <br/>
                </p>
                <p>
                 Due to  Scar tissues in male private organ
                </p>
                <p>
                </p>
                <p>
                 Prolonged Erection (Priapism)  Longer erection more than 4 hours
                </p>
                <p>
                 <br/>
                </p>
                <p>
                 Due to - some medical treatment, injection therapy, cocaine use, sickle cell disease etc

                   3 Yoga Poses To Beat Male Dysfunction
                  </div>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">

                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4046770109">
                   <p>
                    If you are not able to maintain healthy erections during an intimacy and cannot perform well during an intercourse with your wife, then you may be suffering from Erectile Dysfunction. You can practice yoga poses and relieve the condition of male impotence. These yoga poses include:-
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   1. Sarvanga Asana or Shoulder Stand
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    You can perform this yoga pose by lying down in a supine position with your hands on the floor. Inhale and lift your legs simultaneously without bending your knees. Now, apply pressure on your palms and lift your body up as much as possible. Maintain this position for a few seconds and return to original position by bending your knees and bending your body to the floor.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   2. Supine Head Knee Posture
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    Sit straight with your legs in front of you. Bend your right leg near the knee and place the heel firmly under the left thigh. Breathe deeply and bend down over your left leg as you eahale slowly. Grab your toes with hand and bring your head closer to the knee. Remain in the pose for a while and bring your body back to the original position. Do not bend your knee. This pose helps in effective working of reproductive organs.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   3. Khandasana
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    You can perform this pose by sitting with your legs stretched in front of you. Then, bend the knees sideways and bring the heels close towards the male organ. Now, with help of your hands, place the soles of your feet against your navel. Release your hands and keep the palms pressed against one another. Then, slowly lower your legs on the floor. The pose increases your sexual energy.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>

                    Kamagra Jelly is a well-known treatment of male impotence. The jelly enables successful intercourse with your wife. The drug consists of sildenafil citrate, an FDA (Food and Drug Administration) approved ingredient. The jelly ensures smoother, stronger and harder erections during an intimacy.                    </p>

                    There are some side-effects of the jelly which include headache, facial redness, dryness in eyes, blocked nose and mild nausea. The jelly works best as per the advice of a doctor and the side-effects can be decreased. The drug is a good alternative for people, who find difficulty swallowing tablets.                    <p>

                   <p>
                    You can add intimacy in your life with your wife and have better relationship with her in following ways:-
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   You should be aware of and pay attention to your emotions. Many of us have two words to describe our emotions, happiness or anger. There are many emotions that fall in between those words. Become aware of emotions by concentrating on the subject and by being attentive to what really goes on inside you.
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   Become aware of your "true inner self." What are the feelings that strike your mind throughout the day? Where do you feel that you don't match up so you fear being vulnerable? You can evaluate if your way of life has been a false place of safety for you to keep an emotional distance from others because you didnt have time.
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   Evaluation of your past.Take a look to your childhood and consider the emotional connectivity of the family you grew up in. Was it fine to express feelings at your home? Did your family really know one another or were they simply staying as people under a single roof?
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   Be determined to be a "safe" partner for your wife to share her emotions, thoughts, and feelings. If you are characterized by criticism or trying to improve your wife, you will close the door on inviting her to share.
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   Increase the duration of time you spend together as a couple. Intimacy cannot be created without spending time talking not just about how you spent your day, but also how you feel about the events of the day.
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   Deal with conflict swiftly. Don't resort to the silent treatment or pass remarks. Learn to "fight sincerely" by discussing the issue out on the table and dealing with it with dignity. This will help strengthen trust and improve intimacy with your wife.
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   Take help and guidance from a Counselor. You may find that a marriage counselor is helpful in taking you and your spouse into new emotional journey. A few private counseling sessions may help you learn some things about yourself and move from where you are to where you want to be.
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    You can have excitement in your life, but problem occurs when you are not able to maintain erections during an intercourse. Then, you may be suffering from the condition of Erectile Dysfunction. This can lead to divorce, breakup and relationship problems with your wife.                    <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    Kamagra Jellies are available in different flavors such as mint, chocolate, banana, mango, pineapple, orange, vanilla and strawberry. The medicine should be consumed an hour before an intercourse and starts showing effects within 4-6 hours. Kamagra Oral Jelly consists of sildenafil citrate, which belongs to the group of PDE 5 (Phospshodiesterase type 5) vasodilator. The drug helps improve blood supply to the male organ. Kamagra Oral Jelly 100 mg is a new and improved treatment of relieving male impotence. The pill helps have strong, smooth and hard erections and to increase pleasure in your love life.

                    Just like erectile dysfunction, premature ejaculation is common among both young and old men. Relatively, it is more common in young adults, but it is also experienced by some men in older age. There are several factors responsible for this sexual problem including stress, anxiety, the fear to perform in bed, excessive masturbation, extreme stimulation, too long foreplay, inability of vessels to hold blood in the organ, heart problems, diabetes and high blood pressure to name a few. However, the prime reason for ejaculation problems is the inability of arteries to maintain the blood in the male organ.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    Premature ejaculation happens to men in several ways. Some men ejaculate just by thinking about her body, while others ejaculate by touching their organ against her genitals. On the other hand, there is a score of individuals who ejaculate before penetration and leave their lady frustrated in bed. Some men are able to penetrate, but get discharged in just 20 to 25 shots. All these conditions are a form of premature ejaculation, a medical condition of not holding ejaculation for a satisfactory and lasting sex.
                   </p>

                    People with ejaculation disorders are not able to satisfy their love lady in bed as they end up spilling out their semen in just 20 to 25 shots. Keep in mind, women like their men to last longer and perform well during intercourse. Most probably, he or she is likely to prescribe a medicine like kamagra jelly or other sildenafil medicines.

Another major advantage with this medicine is that it dissolves faster and starts acting in just 15 minutes. It is available in jelly form, which makes it an ideal choice for men who dont want to take hard tablets for premature ejaculation or those who just dont like swallowing tablets for sexual problems.

                   <p>
                    Lack of sexual desire as well sexual pleasures have led many happily married couples to divorce. The reason for lack of libido in men can be many such as psychological issues caused by stress and worry from the strain of daily life, depression and mental disorders as bipolar. Medical conditions too affect the sex life for example obesity, high cholesterol, stroke, high blood pressure, diabetes &amp; cancer, among many other reasons. Apart from this, one of the main causes behind low libido is erectile dysfunction. Inability to have arousal leads to the loss of sexual desire. Today, a huge number of men across the world suffer from the inability to have an erection and are looking for an effective solution. To treat this widely faced problem, researchers and doctors have come up with Kamagra 100mg tablets.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    Kamagra Tablets: A Promising Solution for Erectile Dysfunction
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    <br/>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    Kamagra tablet is a new and effective medicine that primarily treats erectile dysfunction to result in satisfactory intercourse. It is based on a clinically-tested formula using FDA approved ingredient called Sildenafil citrate. Kamagra tablets start to show their effect within a few minutes of consumption and stay in body for nearly 4 to 6 hours.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    Cheap Kamagra 100mg tablets are essentially a PDE-5 inhibitor that works by restraining PDE-5 enzyme, which restricts blood supply to the genitals to result in dysfunction. Further, when PDE enzyme is repressed, it promotes the level of cGMP (cyclic guanosine monophosphate) chemical, which relaxes blood vessels and promotes blood flow to the penis. Smooth flow of blood to the penis makes it erect harder and enables one to have satisfactory pleasure in bed.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    Benefits of Using Kamagra Tablets
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    <br/>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    Kamagra tablets are widely demanded for their wide array of benefits, which includes no side-effects, FDA approved ingredient Sildenafil Citrate and results in a few minutes of its consumption. Also, it can be used to treat pulmonary hypertension. Constantly increasing customers are a proof of the effectiveness of these tablets.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    Kamagra tablet are available at the most economical prices whereas other treatments for ED might cost an arm and a leg.. Moreover, these can be conveniently shopped online and received in the comfort of home.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    Directions to Use and Store Kamagra Pills
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    <br/>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    To enjoy the effectiveness of these pills, it is suggested to have a tablet approximately 30-45 minutes prior to sexual intercourse. Consume one tablet a day or in 24 hours only when you wish to desire to engage in sexual pleasure. Also, it is recommended to not to combine these tablets with fatty meals as well as mixing with tobacco, nicotine products, alcohol or with other ED medicines.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    For storage, it is suggested to keep these tablets from the reach of children &amp; pets at a cool and dry place. To suit different health conditions, it is offered in varied dosages and strengths: 25 mg, 50 mg and 100 mg.
                   </p>
                   <p>

         <script type="text/javascript">
          jQuery(document).ready(function() {
  			var siteGuid = 'f3ee344206df0c6d0ae2ac138cf16fc8';
  			var userId = $.cookie("grvinsights");
  			if (userId == null) {
  				userId = "unknown";
  			}
  			var current_url = window.location.href;
  			var limit = 3;
  			var url = 'http://rma-api.gravity.com/v0/site/' + siteGuid + '/user/' + userId + '/stories?current_url=' + encodeURI(current_url) + '&amp;limit=' + parseInt(limit, 10) +"&amp;rec_type=sponsored" + '&amp;c=?';
  			$.ajax({
  			    type: 'GET',
  			    dataType: 'jsonp',
  			    url: url,
  			    success: function (data) {
  			    	if (data.status.httpCode == 200){
  			    		var payload = data.payload;
					var ads = jQuery(".gravity");
					jQuery(payload).each(function (index, article) {
						var adpost = jQuery(jQuery(ads).get(index));
						if (typeof(adpost) != "undefined") {
							// title
							jQuery("h2 a", adpost).attr("href", article.url).text(article.title);
							// image
							var image = jQuery(".post-image", adpost);
							jQuery("a", image).attr("href", article.url);
							jQuery("img", image).data("original", article.image).lazyload({
						    	failure_limit: 20
						    });
							// description
							jQuery(".post-description blockquote", adpost).text(article.summary);
							// domain
							
							var url = document.createElement('a');
							url.href = article.targetUrl;
							jQuery(".post-metas a", adpost).text(url.hostname).attr("href", article.url);
							// show
							adpost.show();
							
							// Is there a post to print?
							var gravityItems = jQuery("#gravity-items");
							if (gravityItems.length &gt; 0) {
								var gravityItem = jQuery("&lt;div class='gravity-item' /&gt;");
								
								// Image
								var gravityImage = jQuery("&lt;div class='gravity-image' /&gt;");
								gravityImage.css({
									backgroundImage: "url('"+article.image+"')"
								});
								gravityItem.append(gravityImage);
								gravityImage.wrap("&lt;a href='"+ article.url+"'  target='_blank' rel='nofollow' /&gt;");
								
								// Title
								var gravityTitle = jQuery("&lt;h3 &gt;"+article.title+"&lt;/h3&gt;");
								gravityItem.append(gravityTitle);
								gravityTitle.wrapInner("&lt;a href='"+ article.url+"' target='_blank' rel='nofollow'/&gt;");
								
								// Source
								var gravitySource = jQuery("&lt;div class='gravity-source'&gt;From &lt;/div&gt;");
								var gravitySourceA = jQuery("&lt;a /&gt;");
								gravitySourceA.attr("href", article.url);
								gravitySourceA.text(url.hostname);
								gravitySourceA.attr("target", "_blank");
								gravitySourceA.attr("rel", "nofollow");
								
								gravitySource.append(gravitySourceA);
								gravityItem.append(gravitySource);
								
								// Track click
								jQuery("a", gravityItem).each(function() {
									jQuery(this).click(function() {
										trackClick("clickOnGravityAds", function() {return true;}, null);
									});
								});
								
								gravityItems.append(gravityItem);
							}
						}
					});
					jQuery("#gravity-items").fadeIn();
  			    	} else {
  			    	}
  			       
  			    },
  			    error: function (e) {
  			    }
  			});
  		});
         </script>

window.twttr.ready(function (twttr) {
	twttr.events.bind('tweet', function(event) {
		var url = jQuery(event.target).parent().attr("data-unshortenUrl");
		var location = jQuery(event.target).parent().attr("data-location");
		trackNativeButtonShare('twitter', location, url);
	});
});

function linkedinShareSuccess(e) {
	var location = jQuery(".linkedin-share-button[data-href='"+e+"']").attr("data-location");
	var url = e;
	trackNativeButtonShare('linkedin', location, url);
}

(function() {
    var po = document.createElement('script'); po.type = 'text/javascript'; po.async = true;
    po.src = 'https://apis.google.com/js/plusone.js';
    var s = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0]; s.parentNode.insertBefore(po, s);
})();
  
  
function googlePlusTouched(e) {
	if (e.state == "on") {
		var url = e.href;
		var location = "bottomOfPost";
		trackNativeButtonShare('google', location, url);
	}
}


function loadSocialWidgetInAPost(post) {
	if (post.length &gt; 0) {
		//facebook
		if (typeof FB != 'undefined') {
			FB.XFBML.parse(jQuery(".share-button-fb",post)[0]);
			post.addClass("loaded-fb");
		}
		//twitter
		if (typeof twttr != 'undefined') {
			jQuery(".share-button-tw a", post).addClass("twitter-share-button");
			twttr.widgets.load(jQuery(".share-button-tw",post)[0]);
			post.addClass("loaded-tw");
		}
		//G+
		if (typeof gapi != 'undefined') {
			gapi.plusone.go(jQuery(".share-button-gp",post)[0]);
			post.addClass("loaded-gp");
		}
	}
}


function loadVisibleSharers() {
	jQuery(".post").each(function(){
		var elt = jQuery(this);
		if (elt.attr("id") == "topic-tags-widget") {
			return;
		}
		if (elt.hasClass("loaded-tw") &amp;&amp; elt.hasClass("loaded-gp") &amp;&amp; elt.hasClass("loaded-fb")) {return;}
		if (elt.isOnScreen()) {
			loadSocialWidgetInAPost(elt);
		}
	});
}

jQuery(window).bind("resize", function(event) {
	loadVisibleSharers();
});

var scrollingChecker = 0;
function onScroll(event) {
	clearTimeout(scrollingChecker);
	scrollingChecker = setTimeout(onStopScrolling, 300);
}

function onStopScrolling() {
	loadVisibleSharers();
}

jQuery(document).bind("scroll", onScroll);
